        <script>
            $_DOMAIN = 'https://tuoitho.mobi';

            $('.clicklogin').on('click', function() {
                $(".login_box").show();
            });
            
            $('#c_loginbox').on('click', function() {
                $(".login_box").hide();
            });
            
            $('.title_group').on('click', function() {
                var a=$(this).parents(".item_group"),b=a.find(".items_character"),c=a.find(".count");
                b.slideToggle(200),c.hasClass("red")?c.removeClass("red"):c.addClass("red");
            });
            
            $(".title_group").on("click",".se-q",function(){
                var a=i(this).parents(".se-c");
                b=a.find(".se-a");
                c=a.find(".se-t");
                b.slideToggle(200);
                c.hasClass("se-o")?c.removeClass("se-o"):c.addClass("se-o");
            });
            
            // Lên đầu trang
            $('#top-page').on('click', function() {
                return $("html, body").animate({scrollTop:0},"slow"),!1;
            });
            
            //Go To Top
            $('.go-to-top').on('click', function () {
                $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: 0}, "slow");
            });
            $(window).on('scroll', function () {
                if ($(window).scrollTop() >= (window.innerHeight * 0.5)) {
                    if (!$('.go-to-top').hasClass('active')) {
            	    $('.go-to-top').addClass('active');
            	};
            	} else {
            	    $('.go-to-top').removeClass('active');
            	};
            });
            		
            // Mở menu ở mobile
            $('.nav-resp').on('click', function() {
                $("#arch-menu").toggleClass("sidblock");
                $(".nav-resp").toggleClass("bi bi-x");
                $(".nav-resp").toggleClass("bi bi-list");
            });
            
            // Mở tìm kiếm ở mobile
            $('.search-resp').on('click', function() {
                $("#form-search-resp").toggleClass("formblock");
                $(".search-resp").toggleClass("active");
            });
            
            // Random truyen
            $('.clickrandom').on('click', function() {
                $('.clickrandom').addClass("loading");
                $.ajax({
                    url : $_DOMAIN + '/report.php',
                    type : 'POST',
                    data : {
                        action : 'random'
                    }, success : function(data) {
                        $('.clickrandom').removeClass("loading");
                        $('#oscuridad').html(data);
                    }, error : function(data) {
                        console.log(data);
                    }
                });
            });
            
            // dang xuat
            $('.logout').on('click', function() {
                $.ajax({
                    url : $_DOMAIN + '/form.php',
                    type : 'POST',
                    data : {
                        action : 'logout'
                    }, success : function(data) {
                        location.reload();
                        console.log(data);
                    }, error : function(data) {
                        location.reload();
                        console.log(data);
                    }
                });
            });
            
            function decodeJwtResponse(token){
                var base64Url = token.split('.')[1];
                var base64 = base64Url.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
                var jsonPayload = decodeURIComponent(window.atob(base64).split('').map(function(c) {
                return '%' + ('00' + c.charCodeAt(0).toString(16)).slice(-2);
                }).join(''));
            
                return JSON.parse(jsonPayload);
            }
    
            function handleCredentialResponse(response) {
                const responsePayload = decodeJwtResponse(response.credential);
                
                $.ajax({
                    url : $_DOMAIN + '/form.php',
                    type : 'POST',
                    data : {
                        id_acc : responsePayload.sub,
                        display_name : responsePayload.name,
                        email : responsePayload.email,
                        avatar : responsePayload.picture,
                        action : 'login'
                    }, success : function(data) {
                        location.reload();
                        console.log(data);
                    }, error : function(data) {
                        location.reload();
                        console.log(data);
                    }
                });
            }
            
            function authenticate() {
                gapi.load('client:auth2', initClient);
            }
    
            function initClient() {
                gapi.client.init({
                    apiKey: 'AIzaSyCVzdMgs82rOyLVKUxOV1Uhp4spqBNtwAY',
                    clientId: '713365941325-1qb3a2b4i7r2msvlcplcinb5bthlokh1.apps.googleusercontent.com',
                    discoveryDocs: ["https://www.googleapis.com/discovery/v1/apis/drive/v3/rest"],
                    scope: 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.metadata.readonly'
                }).then(function () {
                    // Client is initialized, you can now use gapi.client.drive to make requests
                    // Sign in the user
                    gapi.auth2.getAuthInstance().signIn().then(function () {
                        // User is signed in, you can now make authorized requests to Google Drive API
                        var accessToken = gapi.auth2.getAuthInstance().currentUser.get().getAuthResponse().access_token;
                        
                        $.ajax({
                            url : $_DOMAIN + '/form.php',
                            type : 'POST',
                            data : {
                                accessToken : accessToken,
                                action : 'access'
                            }, success : function(data) {
                                location.reload();
                                console.log(data);
                            }, error : function(data) {
                                location.reload();
                                console.log(data);
                            }
                        });
                
                        console.log("Access token:", accessToken);
                        // Now you can use the access token to make requests to the Google Drive API
                    });
                });
            }
